The O

are O
the O
national O

of O

. O

Scouting O
was O
founded O
in O

as O

of O

of O

country O
's O

split O
in O
1971 O
during O

Bangladesh I-MISC

War I-MISC
. O

Following O
its O
independence O
, O

became O

of O
the O
World I-ORG

1974 O
. O

The O
organization O
has O
721,635 O
members O
as O
of O
2004 O
. O

During O

Bangladesh I-MISC
Liberation I-MISC

, O

in O
India I-LOC
. O

Scouting O
has O
grown O
over O

years O
in O
the O
face O
of O
considerable O

. O

Scouts O
are O
involved O
in O
community O
service O
, O
major O
areas O
being O
agriculture O
, O
health O
and O
sanitation O
, O

, O

. O

. O

, O
